{
  "master_prompt": {
    "scene_type": "high-speed cinematic luxury dessert photography",

    "product": {
      "type": "ultra-premium molten chocolate lava cake",

        "quenelle of vanilla bean ice cream",

        "soft rim lighting outlining cake texture",
        "warm directional key light enhancing molten gloss",
        "gentle top light defining ice cream texture",
        "subtle backlight for cinematic depth and separation"
      ]
    },

    "color_palette": {

### 5. Nano Banana Pro 产品组装视频提示

**Author**: [K](https://x.com/ChillaiKalan__)  **Date**: 2026-03-04  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一个超逼真的高端美妆广告视频，展示罐装产品平滑、慢动作的组装过程，并使用上传的图片作为所有元素和构图的精确视觉参考。

![Nano Banana Pro 产品组装视频提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772692199716_5a14z7_HCiGOaaagAA7co3.jpg)

```
Use the uploaded image as the exact visual reference for jar design, label, strawberries, raspberries, flowers, leaves, condensation droplets, red gradient background, and reflective surface.

Camera:
Locked front-facing camera.
No zoom.
No rotation.
No angle change.
Studio composition remains centered.

Style:
Premium beauty commercial.
Smooth assembling sequence.
Ultra realistic.
Slow motion but not dramatic.

Scene – Start (Empty Setup):
Start with an empty red gradient background and glossy reflective surface.
No jar.
No fruits.
No flowers.
No water droplets.

Assembling Sequence:

1. The glass jar base smoothly slides into frame from below and settles perfectly centered.
2. The lid gently lowers from above and aligns perfectly on the jar.
3. Condensation droplets subtly appear on the glass surface as if forming naturally.
4. Raspberries roll in softly from left and right, stopping naturally around the base.
5. Strawberry halves slide into position at the front.
6. Whole strawberries gently drop from above into the open jar top and settle naturally.
7. Small white flowers softly fall into place between the strawberries.
8. Green leaves slide in behind the jar to frame it.
9. Final micro water droplets appear on fruits for freshness effect.

All movements smooth and controlled.
No bouncing.
No exaggerated motion.
No dramatic lighting changes.

Lighting:
Keep original studio lighting.
Deep red background glow remains consistent.
Soft reflections on the glossy surface.

Sound (if supported):
Soft subtle assembling sound design.
Gentle fruit placement sounds.
Light glass contact sound.
No music or very subtle premium ambient tone.

End Frame:
Fully assembled composition exactly matching the reference image.
Everything perfectly arranged.
Hold for 1–2 seconds.
Ultra clean luxury skincare commercial finish.
```

[[Commercial Beauty Ad]]

### 10. 逼真街拍提示词：涩谷复古时尚女孩

**Author**: [オッドアイ白猫ムク【AI副業×AI画像生成】](https://x.com/Sora2LabMuku)  **Date**: 2026-03-03  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana 2 设计的详细逼真图像生成提示，描述了一位身着复古时尚（棒球夹克、芥末色围巾、破洞牛仔裤）的年轻日本女性，在黄昏时分站在涩谷交叉路口路边，以 35mm-50mm 街头摄影美学捕捉。

![逼真街拍提示词：涩谷复古时尚女孩](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772605589795_36rz39_HChPTVcb0AAqmcG.jpg)

```
PROMPT:
Ultra high-resolution photorealistic street photo at dusk (blue hour) in Shibuya, Tokyo, at the famous scramble crossing. Neon signs and city lights glowing in the background with strong bokeh, crowded pedestrians with slight motion blur, cinematic urban atmosphere. A young Japanese woman (around early 20s), small face, natural youthful features, dark brown to black medium bob haircut with straight bangs. She is looking downward with a quiet, slightly melancholic expression, eyes cast down, calm and reserved mood. Full-body shot in a vertical composition, standing near the curb on the sidewalk, relaxed posture with one hand in a pocket, shoulders slightly tucked in.

Outfit: red and beige varsity jacket with white striped ribbing, plain white T-shirt underneath. Thick mustard-yellow knitted scarf wrapped around her neck with visible fringes. Oversized faded wide-leg blue jeans with heavy distressing and large rips around the knees. Red-and-black basketball-style sneakers, black laces. Crosswalk white stripes visible, evening warm light on the pavement, no rain.

Camera & look: 35mm–50mm street photography, f/1.8–f/2.8, shallow depth of field, sharp focus on the subject’s face and upper body, background softly blurred. Natural skin texture (no heavy beauty filter), subtle pores, realistic hair strands. Cinematic color grading (warm highlights, slightly cool shadows), HDR, crisp detail, low noise, 8K quality, vertical 9:16, full body in frame, no cropping.

NEGATIVE PROMPT:
low quality, blurry, out of focus, bad anatomy, deformed body, distorted face, uneven eyes, extra fingers, extra limbs, unnatural joints, plastic skin, over-smoothed skin, AI-looking shine, heavy noise, grain, text, watermark, logo, readable sign text, cropped body, out of frame, overexposed, blown highlights, crushed blacks, anime style, illustration, cartoon
```

### 11. 将照片转换为黑白填色页

**Author**: [Ai Prompts Lab](https://x.com/Aipromptslap)  **Date**: 2026-03-03  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的提示，旨在将现有照片转换为适合儿童的简化黑白涂色页，同时保持构图和相似度，并严格遵守线条、阴影和可打印性规则。

![将照片转换为黑白填色页](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772605583943_9wm648_HCg9u4maUAA5dt6.jpg)
![将照片转换为黑白填色页](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772605583941_rwzc16_HCg9u4mawAQIwmd.jpg)

```
Convert the provided photo into a black and white coloring page. Preserve the original composition, proportions, and recognizable facial features from the original photo.
Style: children's illustration with a soft cartoonish look, inspired by Pixar aesthetics, but simplified for coloring.
Lines: clean, smooth, medium-thickness outlines, clear closed shapes, no broken lines, no sketchiness.
Shading: no gray colors, no shadows, no gradients — outlines only.
Details: simplified but accurate, preserving the recognizability of key objects and expressions, removing unnecessary background.
Faces: expressive, friendly, slightly rounded features, kid-friendly, maintaining likeness.
Background: simplified interior or environmental elements, minimalistic yet readable.
Composition: centered, balanced, with comfortable margins for printing.
Technical requirements:
– clean black lines on a white background
– high contrast
– printable A4 / US Letter format
– suitable for coloring with pencils or markers
No color, no textures, no realism, no photo effects, no hatching, no cross-hatching.
```

[[Line Art Conversion]]

### 12. 超逼真产品渲染，搭配 Holochrome 渐变

**Author**: [Lloyd Creates](https://x.com/lloydcreates)  **Date**: 2026-03-03  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成超逼真 8K 产品渲染图的高度技术性提示。它在灯光（硬边缘光、轮廓光、明暗对比）、材质（拉丝铝、镜面镀铬）和构图（居中、悬浮在纯黑虚空中）方面指定了极致的细节，同时严格禁止常见的摄影元素。

![超逼真产品渲染，搭配 Holochrome 渐变](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772605586143_0xb7bg_HCfukwtWsAAqFSp.jpg)

```
Create a hyper-realistic 8K product render of {argument name="product name" default="[INSERT YOUR PRODUCT HERE]"}

The subject should be perfectly centered and levitating in mid-air, floating in a void with no surface, platform, stand, or floor. Show the full product with zero cropping and visible margins on all sides. 
Use a dynamic macro 45-degree hero angle.

The background must be solid pure black (#000000).

Lighting should feature hard edge lighting with strong rim light highlights. Use a high-contrast chiaroscuro look with thin chromatic aberration along metallic edges. Include reflective caustic light hits and an oily iridescent sheen on polished surfaces.

Color palette:

Background: #000000
Metal highlights: #E0E0E0
Iridescent accents: #4169E1, #FFD700, #FF4500

Materials and textures should combine micro-brushed sandblasted aluminum with mirror-finish chrome. Add subtle prismatic dispersion and thin-film interference along metal curves. Include fine film grain for tactile realism.

Do not include any props or additional objects. 
No light boxes, umbrellas, softboxes, pedestals, cables, tripods, or hands. 
No cropped edges or cut-off parts. 
No text, logos, watermarks, blur, bokeh background, dust, or scratches.

Style reference: Industrial Design meets luxury hardware photography.
```

### 23. 适用于 Nano Banana Pro 和 Google Veo 3.1 的详细视频生成提示

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-03-03  **Language**: ja

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于使用 Nano Banana Pro 生成初始图像，并使用 Google Veo 3.1 生成视频。该提示指定了摄像机角度、构图、光照（逼真的 UGC 风格）、主体表情（平静、略带微笑）、质量（高质量夜间室内视频）、氛围（温暖、明亮、亲密），甚至还有主体的对话和背景音乐。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Video Generation Workflow]] [[Warm Intimate Atmosphere]]

The sides of the box must contain functional doors and windows, with the front-facing side featuring a wide open doorway and visible windows. No side of the box may be removed, cut away, or missing. The box height:width:length ratio is 1:4:7 (the width four times the height). The scene features PRIMARY_ACTIVITY actively interacting with the environment. The structure must be fully integrated into the box material itself — not a room inserted inside, not a display frame, not a cutaway model. The ground floor must be constructed from the same material as the box exterior.

A mezzanine or upper level is built above with structural elements attached directly to the box walls and connected via STAIR_TYPE. The inside of the open lid functions as the vaulted ceiling decorated with CEILING_DETAILS.
DETAILS:
Intricately carved ornate box styled according to THEME_MATERIAL_STYLE. Exterior ornamentation must continue logically into interior architecture. Doors and windows must be precisely cut into the box sides following decorative carving patterns. Include believable miniature structural joins where beams meet the container walls. Include ultra-fine theme-specific props such as PROP_LIST. Include floating dust, micro-surface wear, tactile handcrafted realism, and environmental storytelling details.
STYLE:
Ultra-realistic cinematic miniature diorama photography, museum-grade handcrafted realism, extreme macro detail, physically believable materials, strong architectural integration of container and structure.

### 60. 夏洛克·福尔摩斯华丽橱柜立体模型提示

```
Variable Guide
1. OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME = Scenes from Adventures of Sherlock Holmes by Arthur Conan Doyle, in the order in which they are presented in the book
2. CUPBOARD_BASE_MATERIAL = 
3. CUPBOARD_LINING_MATERIAL = 
4. RACK_MATERIAL =

7. TOP_SHELF_SCENE = [Describe specific actions of miniature figures defining the scene]
8. MIDDLE_SHELF_SCENE = [Describe specific actions of miniature figures defining the scene]
9. BOTTOM_SHELF_SCENE = [Describe specific actions of miniature figures defining the scene]
10. LIGHTING = 
11. CAMERA_ANGLE = A straight-on, front-facing view, captured from a moderately high angle looking distinctly downward.
12. ASPECT_RATIO = 3:4

Generation Directives
(Note: If any variable is left blank, intelligently infer the most appropriate detail based on the OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME)

Directive 1: Framing & Composition (Highest Priority)
A direct, front-facing photograph captured from CAMERA_ANGLE. The composition must perfectly center the open display structure, looking down at a distinct angle into the shelves to clearly reveal the floor plates and top-down depth of the miniature objects within the dioramas, while ensuring the exterior side panels remain completely hidden. The entire free-standing structure must be completely visible with negative space around it against a simple background. The aspect ratio is 3:4.

Directive 2: The Main Structure (Strict Constraints)
Render the image in the style of ART_STYLE. The central object is a highly detailed, permanently open-front curio display structure. It must not possess doors, hinges, or door frames of any kind. The exterior is constructed from CUPBOARD_BASE_MATERIAL and detailed with ORNAMENTATION_STYLE. The interior back wall is lined with CUPBOARD_LINING_MATERIAL, and the individual shelves are made of RACK_MATERIAL.

Directive 3: The Miniature Dioramas & Figures
The structure houses a cohesive miniature world divided across three shelves, adhering to the OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME. Crucially, each shelf must contain miniature figures engaged in a specific narrative action.
* Top Shelf: Miniature figures are depicted [TOP_SHELF_SCENE].
* Middle Shelf: Miniature figures are depicted [MIDDLE_SHELF_SCENE].
* Bottom Shelf: Miniature figures are depicted [BOTTOM_SHELF_SCENE].
Ensure the scale clearly reads as miniature dioramas housed within a furniture piece.

Directive 4: Atmosphere & Lighting
The scene is illuminated by LIGHTING. The lighting should cast appropriate micro-shadows within each shelf to emphasize the depth, the figures, and the miniature scale of the dioramas.

{
  "vibe_title_en": "Gravity-Defying Alchemist Atelier",

The composition is perfectly symmetrical. The subject stares forward with intense, ritualistic focus, hair slightly messy, wearing a deconstructed white couture shirt with sleeves rolled up, exuding raw energy. SURREAL ELEMENT: The clutter is experiencing a localized gravity failure; droplets of liquid gold, shards of mirrors, and clouds of setting powder are frozen in mid-air around the subject, captured as if they are high-end practical effects. Lighting is clinical and symmetrical: dual large soft-boxes from both sides creating even, shadow-less, porcelain skin tones. Cinematic color grading with rich ambers, dusty rose, and clinical whites.",
  "meta": {

### 78. 高对比度单色肖像提示

**Author**: [K](https://x.com/ChillaiKalan__)  **Date**: 2026-03-02  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细的提示，用于生成一张高对比度黑白艺术工作室肖像，要求精确复制参考图像中主体的身份、面部特征和表情。它指定了复杂的布光设置（低调、定向柔光箱）和构图（紧凑的垂直裁剪、“思想者”姿势）。

![高对比度单色肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772519713802_rhqp8h_HCZJGaDbMAExqCv.jpg)
![高对比度单色肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772519713839_mqoi7e_HCZJGana4AADgjR.jpg)
![高对比度单色肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772519713818_sn66fu_HCZJGaGbIAAtx9W.jpg)

```
Create a striking, ultra-detailed, high-contrast monochrome lack-and-white) portrait based on the uploaded reference image. The subject’s facial structure and identity must match the reference precisely accurately replicate bone structure, eye shape, nose proportions, jawline definition, beard density (if present), hairline, and overall facial symmetry. Maintain authentic skin texture and natural features without artificial smoothing.
Subject & Expression A mature, confident man with a strong facial structure and deep-set eyes looking directly into the camera. Expression should be serious, contemplative, and quietly authoritative. Preserve natural skin details such as pores, fine lines, and subtle texture for realism. The gaze should feel focused and introspective, not aggressive.
Facial Hair (Adaptive)
If facial hair is present in the reference image, replicate it exactly — density, length, shape, and edges. Maintain natural tonal variation (including salt-and-pepper graying if applicable). Beard lines should be clean and structured.

If clean-shaven, preserve realistic skin texture and jaw definition.
Hairstyle (Adaptive)
Match the hairstyle from the reference image exactly — volume, direction, hairline, and texture. Hair should look natural with visible strand detail and subtle specular highlights from overhead directional lighting.
Pose
Classic “thinker” pose. One hand raised to the chin with thumb along the jawline and index finger slightly curled. Knuckles and tendons subtly defined for realism. Hand in sharp focus with visible skin texture and natural tonal gradation.
🔥 Lighting & Technical Style (Accurately Customized)
Low-key fine-art studio photography with controlled high-contrast sculpting.
• Primary key light positioned slightly above eye level and slightly toward the viewer’s left, angled downward to create strong top-plane highlights.

• Light is soft but directional (large softbox or diffused beauty dish), producing crisp edge definition without harsh clipping.

• Strong highlight concentration on forehead center, nose bridge, upper cheekbones, beard texture, and the top planes of the hand.

• Subtle shadow shaping under the brow ridge and cheekbones to enhance bone structure.

• The shadow side of the face remains deep but not fully crushed — maintaining controlled midtone detail.

• Minimal fill light from front-center to retain facial symmetry while preserving depth.

• Very subtle rim separation along hair edges and outer shoulder to prevent blending into background.

• Catchlights centered and natural — small, soft rectangular reflection in both eyes.

• Background is fully black with zero visible texture, absorbing all spill light.
Contrast ratio should be high but refined — not blown highlights, not muddy blacks. Clean tonal roll-off.
Composition
Tight vertical head-and-shoulders crop (portrait orientation, 4:5 ratio recommended). Subject centered symmetrically for a formal, balan
```

[[Black And White Photography]] [[Identity Reference Match]]

### 83. Nano Banana Pro 的现代室内生活方式肖像提示

```
Create an ultra-realistic, cinematic 8K image with high-contrast dramatic lighting and a photo-real digital painting aesthetic-use face reference exactly. The man is shown in a full-body side profile facing right, his face and hairstyle copied perfectly with no alterations He wears modern casual streetwear; a light grey crewneck t-shirt, light neutral cargo pants, light-colored high-top boots, and a watch on his left wrist. His posture is slightly slumped, head bowed, eyes looking downward, hands relaxed at his sides, conveying deep introspection and sorrow. Nearly half of his body is dissolving into extremely thick, cloud-like grey smoke filled with glowing yellow dust particles. His left arm, shoulder, torso, legs, and part of his hair become transparent as they break into luminous particles, suggesting active disintegration Behind and partially surrounding him is a massive glowing crescent (C-shaped) energy aura, emitting fiery golden-white plasma light. This aura acts as a powerful rim and backlight, highlighting the smoke, dust, and silhouette. The setting is minimal and stark: a concrete or desolate paved surface meeting a heavily overcast sky. The color palette is nearly monochrome greys and whites, contrasted by intense amber-gold glow, Shallow depth of field, glow/bloom lighting, particle dispersion, cinematic composition, emotional and dramatic atmosphere.

### 107. 48 面板工作室表情联系表

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-03-01  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 Nano Banana Pro 提示，用于生成一个 6x8 网格（48 个面板）的联系表。目标是保持成年男性主体的确切身份、构图和背景，同时生成 48 种不同的面部表情和最少的手势，确保所有面板之间具有极高的一致性，以呈现干净的编辑肖像风格。

![48 面板工作室表情联系表](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433505320_mdycka_HCWmvwKXkAEpArG.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "studio_expression_contact_sheet_6x8_clean",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.0_48_PANEL_FACE_LOCK"
    },
    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "very_high",
      "preserve_identity": true,
      "preserve_facial_features": true,
      "preserve_hairstyle": true,
      "preserve_wardrobe": true,
      "notes": "Create a 6x8 grid (48 panels) studio expression contact sheet. Same adult male identity in every panel. White seamless background. Head-and-shoulders framing locked. Only facial expressions and minimal hand gestures change. No text, no watermark, no logos."
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 8,
        "cols": 6,
        "gutter": "thin_white",
        "outer_border": "none",
        "panel_consistency": "extreme"
      },
      "sharpness": "studio_crisp",

### 108. 华丽盒子立体模型主提示（莫卧儿大厅内部）

**Author**: [Artingent](https://x.com/artingent)  **Date**: 2026-03-01  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂、结构化的主提示，用于在一个华丽的盒子内生成一个超逼真的微缩立体模型，并使用自动主题系统。盒子本身构成了大理石莫卧儿宫殿内部的建筑结构，详细描述了结构整合、材料风格、照明和微缩模型的真实感。

![华丽盒子立体模型主提示（莫卧儿大厅内部）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433489043_019tka_HCWlPr4bQAAtbWl.jpg)

```
Scene:
ORNATE BOX DIORAMA — AUTO-THEME MASTER PROMPT
========================
SMART VARIABLE GUIDE
THEME_LOCATION = {argument name="theme location" default="Marble Mughal Hall Interior"}
AUTO RULES:
• If THEME_LOCATION is filled → automatically infer:
PRIMARY_ACTIVITY
STAIR_TYPE
CEILING_DETAILS
THEME_MATERIAL_STYLE 
PROP_LIST
THEME_LIGHT_SOURCE
BASE_MATERIAL_COLOR
THEME_PALETTE
FOCAL_SUBJECT
All inferred values must be logically consistent with THEME_LOCATION.
• If THEME_LOCATION is blank → first invent a visually rich miniature environment theme, assign it to THEME_LOCATION, then automatically infer all other variables from it.
• Always prioritize strong environmental storytelling, believable materials, and handcrafted miniature realism when inferring values.
========================
SUBJECT:
A two-level miniature THEME_LOCATION where the ornate open box itself forms the architecture, the base container acting as the full ground floor chamber with the box walls serving directly as the structural walls. The sides of the box must contain functional doors and windows, with the front-facing side featuring a wide open doorway and visible windows. No side of the box may be removed, cut away, or missing. The box height:width:length ratio is 1:4:7 (the width four times the height). The scene features PRIMARY_ACTIVITY actively interacting with the environment. The structure must be fully integrated into the box material itself — not a room inserted inside, not a display frame, not a cutaway model. The ground floor must be constructed from the same material as the box exterior.
ENVIRONMENT:
The base of the ornate box forms the ground floor surface and foundation. Its interior sides transform into the architectural walls containing carved doorways and window openings seamlessly cut into the box sides and aligned with exterior ornamentation. A mezzanine or upper level is built above with structural elements attached directly to the box walls and connected via STAIR_TYPE. The inside of the open lid functions as the vaulted ceiling decorated with CEILING_DETAILS.
DETAILS:
Intricately carved ornate box styled according to THEME_MATERIAL_STYLE. Exterior ornamentation must continue logically into interior architecture. Doors and windows must be precisely cut into the box sides following decorative carving patterns. Include believable miniature structural joins where beams meet the container walls. Include ultra-fine theme-specific props such as PROP_LIST. Include floating dust, micro-surface wear, tactile handcrafted realism, and environmental storytelling details.
STYLE:
Ultra-realistic cinematic miniature diorama photography, museum-grade handcrafted realism, extreme macro detail, physically believable materials, strong architectural style integration of container and structure.
LIGHTING:
Primary lighting motivated by THEME_LIGHT_SOURCE combined with subtle environmental secondary lighting entering through box windows
```

### 109. 《海底两万里》华丽盒式立体模型提示词

**Author**: [Artingent](https://x.com/artingent)  **Date**: 2026-03-01  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化、变量驱动的提示模板，用于生成一个基于儒勒·凡尔纳《海底两万里》的华丽盒式立体模型。该提示使用变量来描述主题、材料、风格以及三个搁板上的场景，并包含关于框架、构图和照明的严格指令，以确保呈现出微缩模型的审美效果。

```
Variable Guide
1. OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME = Scenes from the book  Twenty Thousand leagues under the sea  by Jules Verne, in the order in which they are presented in the book

3. CUPBOARD_LINING_MATERIAL =

5. ORNAMENTATION_STYLE = [e.g., Gothic carved wood, Art Deco brass, Elven interlaced vines]
6. ART_STYLE = Hyper-Realistic Render
7. TOP_SHELF_SCENE = [Describe specific actions of miniature figures defining the scene]
8. MIDDLE_SHELF_SCENE = [Describe specific actions of miniature figures defining the scene]
9. BOTTOM_SHELF_SCENE = [Describe specific actions of miniature figures defining the scene]
10. LIGHTING = 
11. CAMERA_ANGLE = A straight-on, front-facing view, captured from a moderately high angle looking distinctly downward.
12. ASPECT_RATIO = 3:4

Generation Directives
(Note: If any variable is left blank, intelligently infer the most appropriate detail based on the OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME)

Directive 1: Framing & Composition (Highest Priority)
A direct, front-facing photograph captured from CAMERA_ANGLE. The composition must perfectly center the open display structure, looking down at a distinct angle into the shelves to clearly reveal the floor plates and top-down depth of the miniature objects within the dioramas, while ensuring the exterior side panels remain completely hidden. The entire free-standing structure must be completely visible with negative space around it against a simple background. The aspect ratio is 3:4.

Directive 2: The Main Structure (Strict Constraints)
Render the image in the style of ART_STYLE. The central object is a highly detailed, permanently open-front curio display structure. It must not possess doors, hinges, or door frames of any kind. The exterior is constructed from CUPBOARD_BASE_MATERIAL and detailed with ORNAMENTATION_STYLE. The interior back wall is lined with CUPBOARD_LINING_MATERIAL, and the individual shelves are made of RACK_MATERIAL.

Directive 3: The Miniature Dioramas & Figures
The structure houses a cohesive miniature world divided across three shelves, adhering to the OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME. Crucially, each shelf must contain miniature figures engaged in a specific narrative action.
* Top Shelf: Miniature figures are depicted [TOP_SHELF_SCENE].
* Middle Shelf: Miniature figures are depicted [MIDDLE_SHELF_SCENE].
* Bottom Shelf: Miniature figures are depicted [BOTTOM_SHELF_SCENE].
Ensure the scale clearly reads as miniature dioramas housed within a furniture piece.

Directive 4: Atmosphere & Lighting
The scene is illuminated by LIGHTING. The lighting should cast appropriate micro-shadows within each shelf to emphasize the depth, the figures, and the miniature scale of the dioramas.

### 148. 浮世绘与工业融合的写实肖像

**Author**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp)  **Date**: 2026-03-01  **Language**: ja

> 一个复杂的图像生成提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro、Nano Banana 2、GPT Image 1.5 和 Seedream 5，重点是一个融合了都市、工业和浮世绘（日本木版画）元素的超写实肖像，具有详细的纹理、几何形状以及在面部工作的微型浮世绘工匠。

![浮世绘与工业融合的写实肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433524876_ifezi5_HCPtwZzbEAgbhPU.jpg)
![浮世绘与工业融合的写实肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433524862_lclvve_HCPtv7PbEAYFXA0.jpg)
![浮世绘与工业融合的写实肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433524874_kctj4r_HCPtv0QbEAEY63E.jpg)
![浮世绘与工业融合的写实肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433525445_na6ocm_HCPtw5zbYAAMCF-.jpg)

```
添付画像の女性をモデルとする。横顔のポートレート。左向きの横顔で、クールで知的な表情。バストアップ構図。

女性の顔と肌は完全にフォトリアルな写真品質を維持する。これは最優先事項であり、イラスト調やアニメ調にならない。毛穴、産毛、まつ毛の一本一本、耳の軟骨の透け感まで見える超高精細な質感。

背景と装飾要素はアーバンとインダストリアルと浮世絵の融合。画面全体にグリッド線と計測線が走っているが、そのグリッドの一部が葛飾北斎の波の曲線に変形している。直線的な設計図の線が、ある地点から急に波頭のうねりへと変貌する。数値やスケール表記が縦書きの和文と混在している。

背景に配置された鋭い幾何学的な三角形やラインは藍色で、その藍は浮世絵の藍摺りと同じ深い青。三角形の内部には木版画の波模様や渦巻き文様が透けて見える。幾何学と浮世絵の文様が一つの画面で共存している。

ミニチュアサイズの人々が女性の顔や輪郭の上で作業している。江戸時代の木版画の彫師と摺師で、小さな彫刻刀で版木を彫り、バレンで和紙に摺っている。浮世絵の職人たちは藍色の着物を着ている。小さな足場と梯子が顔の輪郭に沿って架けられている。

女性の横顔の輪郭線は、ある部分はシャープなデジタルのベクター線、別の部分は墨と筆による浮世絵の輪郭線になっている。二つの線描技法が一人の顔の上で交差している。

インクのスプラッターと飛沫が画面全体に散っているが、黒いインクの飛沫に混じって藍色の墨の飛沫と朱色の飛沫が混在している。グランジテクスチャはコンクリートの壁の質感と和紙の繊維の質感が重なり合っている。

画面内に文字、テキスト、タイポグラフィ、日本語の文字列、落款印、印鑑、ハンコ、署名は一切含まない。

照明はコントラスト強めのドラマチックな陰影。画面左からの硬い光で横顔の輪郭がはっきりとした明暗で浮かび上がる。フィルムグレイン。超高解像度。シャープ。アートポスター風。
```

[[Japanese Woodblock Print]]

### 151. Vlog 风格时尚视频提示

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-03-01  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于使用 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张静态图像，然后使用 Google Veo 3.1 将其转换为视频。该提示旨在创建一段逼真、亲密、高质量的视频，采用 Vlog 风格拍摄，内容是一位女性正在讨论她的时尚。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Vlog Aesthetic]]

### 152. 蝙蝠侠喜剧电影截图提示

Clean symmetrical composition with the bottle perfectly sharp in focus, shallow depth of field, highly detailed textures on water, stone, glass, and foliage. Aesthetic blends luxury fragrance advertising with ethereal nature fantasy, color palette dominated by fresh greens, soft neutrals, and crystal-clear water tones. Photorealistic 8K quality, hyper-detailed textures, premium editorial finish, high dynamic range, professional 85mm lens feel.
```

### 179. 使用 ControlNet 制作逼真的抓拍生活照

**Author**: [Marco](https://x.com/maarcoofdezz)  **Date**: 2026-02-28  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术化的 JSON 提示词，用于 Nano Banana Pro，指定一张年轻女性身穿黄色比基尼，坐在半户外酒吧区藤椅上的写实抓拍生活照。关键在于，它包含了详细的 ControlNet 参数（OpenPose 用于坐姿，MiDaS 用于深度控制）以及一个广泛的负面提示词，以确保高质量和真实感。

![使用 ControlNet 制作逼真的抓拍生活照](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772346669636_hb51ji_HCQvvzLaYAAdQnH.jpg)

```
